It's all fun & games. Until it isn't. Developed over the course of a year, this piece is inspired after time spent playing with our own children. While we certainly take things to an extreme, we believe there is an underlying truth that is interesting to think about. We hope you enjoy it!</p>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/435789152\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1680px;margin:auto;\">\n<div style=\"left: 0; width: 100%; height: 0; position: relative; Array body\"><p>Good design for me is all about simplicity. I know that term can be interpreted in so many different ways. For me at the top of the list is simplicity of the function, most inevitably that will result in the reduction of the form. In this post I would love to focus on form alone and feature the beautiful work of <a href=\"http://www.gilhuybrecht.com/\">Gil Huybrecht</a>, a designer and skateboarder from Belgium. Gil has an awesome portfolio of minimalist looking website designs that make me want to redesign all my sites using his work as reference.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><a   <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sci-fi-cyberpunk-inspired-branding-paradigmal\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/6b9cdf99671683.5f026b94cd8ff.jpg\" width=\"1920\" height=\"1280\" alt=\"Sci-fi & Cyberpunk inspired Branding for Paradigmal\" title=\"Sci-fi & Cyberpunk inspired Branding for Paradigmal\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>07.23.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://sabbath.mx/\">Sabbath Studio</a> is a branding studio based Monterrey, Mexico. They shared a branding project wholly inspired by Dystopian Futures, Cyberpunk, Sci-fi / Neo-noir Cult Films & Anime themed aesthetics by client request. Let's just mention that again: 'by client request'. This is so cool and the result is just perfect and true representation of that cult era that we dearly love. Even though it's branding, I just enjoy the small details like the 'glitchy style' logo, the grid, colors, and let's not forget about the sublime photography work by <a href=\"http://instagram.com/weroalmaguer\">Wero Almaguer</a>. This pure and hope you will like it too.</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://sabbath.mx/\">https://sabbath.mx/</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/sabbathstudio\">https://www.behance.net/sabbathstudio</a></li>\n</ul><blockquote>The concept is centered on the perception of reality & the endless possibilities as creators of stories: pleasure, pain, joy, frustration, romance, optimism. The Grid is a representation of the possible & the tangible, the hidden miracles beyond the lens. A passport to the unknown, what's not yet made but it will be.</blockquote>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/04b14e100752659.5f16d927a3887.png\" width=\"1400\" height=\"960\" alt=\"Neumorphism icons inspired by macOS Big Sur\" title=\"Neumorphism class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Neumorphism or shall we say Skeuomorphism is a hot topic in UI trends. For the past months we have been talking, debating, and even more since the release announcement of the <a href=\"https://www.apple.com/macos/big-sur-preview/\">macOS Big Sur</a> coming this fall. Why? Because it's cool! One thing, I do like about this 'style' is the craft that goes into an icon design. Something we have neglected since everything is 'flat' nowadays. I do like this shift, obviously there will be debates all sorts of things but why not. Happy to share the work of <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/ax_\">Song hojong</a>, a designer based in Seoul, Korea. He did his interpretation of what is Neumorphism inspired by macOS Big Sur, let's take a look!</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/smile-inducing-miniature-art-tatsuya-tanaka\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_tanaka.png\" width=\"1186\" height=\"814\" alt=\"Smile Inducing Miniature Art by Tatsuya Tanaka\" title=\"Smile Inducing Miniature Art by Tatsuya Tanaka\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/ibby\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/ibby\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">ibby</a>07.22.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>We’ve featured the work of the oh so creative <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/tanaka_tatsuya/\">Tatsuya Tanaka</a> before and we’re happy to share more of his art with you in a time when we could all use a little cheer. Tatsuya is a master at taking your everyday objects and creating a whimsical miniature scene that we just can’t get over. Be it surgical masks that we all now know too well, the recently coveted roll of toilet paper or a hairbrush, an object that may be currently relegated to the bottom of your drawer, Tanaka creatively gives these objects a whole new life. His work is then placed into a <a href=\"https://miniature-calendar.com/about/\">“miniature calendar”</a> collection depicting diorama style figures. Check out some of our recent favorites below and be sure to view the original post by our lovely contributor, Gisele Muller, <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/everyday-miniature-life-tatsuya-tanaka\">here</a>. </p>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://www.instagram.com/p/CBZdLZ6hF90\">\n<div PDT</time></p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n<script async=\"\" src=\"https://www.instagram.com/embed.js\"></script></div>\n</div>\n\n<h3>More ABOUT TATSUYA TANAKA</h3>\n\n<p>Miniature and resemblance artist. Born in Kumamoto Prefecture in 1981. In 2011, he began creating a “MINIATURE CALENDAR”, a form of art that sees him use alternative items to recreate everyday things in miniature form. Since then, he has been updating and uploading content to present online on a daily basis. His exhibition, “MINIATURE LIFE Exhibition: Tatsuya Tanaka’s World of Resemblance”, which is being held both domestically and internationally, has had a total of over 1,000,000 visitors (as of November 2019). As part of his main job, he designed the title sequence for the 2017 NHK serial TV drama, <a href=\"https://www.nhk.or.jp/hiyokko/hiyokko2/special/special3/\">Hiyokko</a>, and the movie used for <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=m1gb02ckHQc\">the opening of the Nihonbashi Takashimaya S.C. department store</a>. He currently has over 2,500,000 followers on <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/tanaka_tatsuya/\">Instagram</a> (as of June 2020). Some of his works include “<a href=\"https://www.amazon.co.jp/dp/4880653284/\">MINIATURE LIFE</a>“, “<a href=\"https://www.amazon.co.jp/dp/4880653810/\">MINIATURE LIFE 2</a>“, “<a href=\"https://www.amazon.co.jp/dp/4865050779/\">Small Wonders</a>“, and “<a href=\"https://www.amazon.co.jp/dp/409682318X\">MINIATURE TRIP IN JAPAN</a>“</p>\n</div><div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a  <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/post-covid-19-signage-design-conscious-workplace\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/Ellie_Pinney_covid_sign_wash_hands.jpg\" width=\"2500\" height=\"1667\" alt=\"Post COVID-19 Signage for the Design-Conscious Workplace \" title=\"Post COVID-19 Signage for the Design-Conscious Workplace \" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/ibby\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/ibby\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">ibby</a>07.23.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>The global pandemic has upended our work life by altering how and where we do our jobs. Seeing a gap in the COVID-19 signage market, <a href=\"https://www.elliepinneydesign.com/portfolio/covid-19-signs\">Ellie Pinney</a> has created a series of thoughtful and considered signs for the design-conscious workplace – complete with tracked-out letters that reflect our new 'socially distanced' world. While the thought of returning to business as usual seems unimaginable right now, we're hopeful for a return to some semblance of normalcy eventually and we're loving Ellie's take on keeping staff and visitors safe with an added touch of (much-needed) lightness. These signage tips are great for employers returning to existing spaces that are looking for inexpensive yet beautifully designed solutions to ensure employees feel safe in the post-COVID office space. </p>\n\n<p>Are you re-opening your office and looking for some smart COVID signs? Ellie is offering designs delivered straight to your inbox as a fully scalable graphic that can be printed or turned into cut vinyl/transfers with a little help from a professional printer. If you're after something more bespoke Ellie can alter the color and/or typeface to fit with your brand for a small additional fee. Learn more <a href=\"https://www.elliepinneydesign.com/portfolio/covid-19-signs\">here</a>. </p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>07.20.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Escuro in Portuguese means dark, blackish or closer to black than white., Escuro is also the name of the new set of Lightroom CC presets created with the intent of turning photos of ocean water in its various states into a minimalistic image. Photography has always been a hobby and a passion for me. I am more of an enthusiast, so the thrilling of learning is present at every click of the shutter.</p>\n\n<p>Back to Escuro, the presets effect is achieved by reducing the brightness and increasing the contrast of the highlights that really matter. It's also a common effect used in motion design and other graphics, like the Imagine Entertainment logo that is animated before movies. As a fan of movies, that inspired me to create this preset to improve the tons of photos of waves and ocean I have taken.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full\"><a href=\"https://gum.co/ysqMCN\"><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/xQX_TOYJUmRpQIGmXWVdD3WS3CrMs-SC2E4lj9DYkH32teB5S2uArqIDLEEB59iIIe5MXOvxgQQYnlRkh4FBfb-isl1o_Q4f3B0fNhgtc-B5dyZVQXijNjlZFzG4gtST0wNl8lO3\" /></a></div>\n\n<h3>What's included</h3>\n\n<p>There are 4 different presets: e1, e2, e3, e4. Self-therapy\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/illustration-ease-ones-mind-designers-self-therapy\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/389591E8-B9EE-43FD-922E-CA1B58C29EAA.jpeg\" width=\"1099\" height=\"778\" alt=\"Illustration to Ease One’s Mind - Designer’s Self-therapy\" title=\"Illustration to Ease One’s Mind - Designer’s Self-therapy\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>07.21.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/orlinska\">Aga Lut</a> is a freelance graphic designer. To ease her mind and to relax after her commercial work, she started to illustrate. “I used to illustrate people a lot, but I’ve grown bored of it.” - she says.  One of the main reasons was that she felt she was lacking her own unique style; many illustrators do something similar, and maybe it’s a good opportunity to experiment. So she said goodbye to digital painting and started her adventure with vectors. Quite a rewarding one, she adds.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>I missed painting on canvas a bit, but I definitely didn’t want to get dirty nor had I space for all that gear, so I started to wonder: how can I convert a bit of painting to vectors, not as a digitalized brushes, but in a modern way? I came up with simple shading which reminded me of strong brush strokes on canvas. I developed a geometrical style of portraying animals. And started to talk about my feelings through it. My illustrations are mostly a form of self-therapy.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<h2>Illustration</h2>\n\n<p> </p>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img The Wallpaper of the Week is happening again due to the incredible demand and pressure from myself and Francois hah! Jokes aside. We have been seeing some really great work, plus taking some good pictures that we think might be great for your phone, tablet or computer wallpapers.</p>\n\n<p>For this edition we have a photo that I’ve taken in Lake Tahoe back in February. It was before the whole craziness of Covid-19. This photo was edited in Lightroom using my new preset <a href=\"https://fabiosasso.com/products/escuro/\">Escuro</a>.
